# <a name="edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin"></a><span data-ttu-id="ff74b-102">Documents informatisés EDIFACT APERAK-IFTRIN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff74b-102">EDIFACT Transaction Sets APERAK-IFTRIN</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="ff74b-103">Cette rubrique répertorie les documents informatisés EDIFACT pris en charge par [!INCLUDE[prague](../includes/prague-md.md)].</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff74b-103">This topic lists the EDIFACT transaction sets that are supported by [!INCLUDE[prague](../includes/prague-md.md)].</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="ff74b-104">Les documents informatisés suivants y sont détaillés :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff74b-104">The following transaction sets are contained in this topic:</span></span>

-   [<span data-ttu-id="ff74b-107">Transaction jeux cntcnd de documents-CONAPW</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff74b-107">Transaction Sets CNTCND-CONAPW</span></span>](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#cntcnd)

-   [<span data-ttu-id="ff74b-109">Jeux de transactions documents-CREMUL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff74b-109">Transaction Sets COPARN-CREMUL</span></span>](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#coparn)  
  
-   [<span data-ttu-id="ff74b-110">Transaction jeux cuscar de documents-DEBREC</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff74b-110">Transaction Sets CUSCAR-DEBREC</span></span>](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#cuscar)  
  
-   [<span data-ttu-id="ff74b-111">Transaction jeux delfor de documents-DOCADV</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff74b-111">Transaction Sets DELFOR-DOCADV</span></span>](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#delfor)
